name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Deluxe Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in November 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted November 25, 2023
msg:I often travel for business, and this hotel has a very high cost-effectiveness among all the hotels I have stayed in. The overall hardware and software are good, and the buffet dinner and breakfast are great, which is a bit beyond my expectations. The attitude of the front desk is also very good, and I have to give it five points for these. However, there are some places where the flaws do not outweigh the merits, and the management is a bit lacking. I hope it will continue to improve.
The parking lot is very cramped at night, with few parking spaces, unclear diversion signs, and a lot of construction waste and materials on the roof and underground car aisle.
The anti-smoke sand at the elevator entrance has obviously not been taken care of for a long time, and it has all lumped.
The window of the room is a little degummed, resulting in a sense of air leakage at night.
There is a desk in the room, but no desk lamp.
There is no spare bedding in the room. I learned from the front desk that there should be some, but the waiter is very good and delivered it quickly after asking.
There are coffee cups, but no coffee.
The toilet door cannot be locked
The most wanted to complain is why there is a toilet paper box that cannot be opened. It is super embarrassing to sit on the toilet and look at this box that cannot be opened.
